DU BSHAD PA LTAR DANG, RGYUD SDE 'OG MA'I DBANG RDZOGS KYI BAR
LA 'OG MA'I DAM TSIG GONG DU DRANGS PA RNAMS BSHAD NA LEGS SAM
SNYAM NAS 'DIR

BKOD PAS SKABS DANG SBYAR LA BLA MA DANG SLOB MA THAMS CAD NYES
PAS MA GOS PAR DBANG BSKUR BA DANG NYAN PA'I PHAN YON 'GRUB PA'I
PHYIR 'BAD 'TSAL LO, ,SMRAS PA, 'JIGS MED ZHABS DANG DHAR PAn AA
TZA RYA'I, ,GZHUNG LAS BSHAD PA'I SLOB MAR DBANG SKUR

TSUL, ,'CHAD PA'I NGAG 'DON YI GER BKOD PA MANG, ,'GA' ZHIG RANG
GI PHYOGS ZHEN AA 'THES PAS, ,BLA MA GONG MA'I DKYIL CHOG PHYAG
LEN GYI, ,RGYAS 'GEB SKABS THOB MIN PAR BYAS PA DANG, ,'GA' ZHIG
HA CANG BSDUS PAS LAG TU BLANG, ,DKA' BAR

MTHONG NAS TSUL 'DIR NGAL BA BSTEN, ,'DIR NI PAn CHEN GNYIS KYI
RGYA GZHUNG LAS, ,JI LTAR GSUNG BA'I DNGOS GZHI CHA TSANG ZHING,
,DBANG LA DBANG BRDA' 'PHROD PA GAL CHE BAR, ,GSUNG PAS RANG
RANG SKABS SU BRDA SPROD TSUL, ,'JAM MGON BLA MA'I

LEGS PAR BSHAD PA LAS, ,BSKANG STE PHYAG LEN MTSAN LDAN BLA MA
YI, ,JI LTAR MDZAD PA'I MTHONG BA BRGYUD PA BZHIN, ,BYA BA'I
TSUL RNAMS LAG TU BLANG BDER BKOD, ,PHYOGS LHUNG LING THOG 'THUG
PO'I BSGRIB PA YI, ,SPYAN GYI 'DI LA GZIGS PAR

MI SPRO YANG, ,GZUR GNAS RNAM DPYOD RAB TU DANGS BA YI, ,SPYAN
GYI NGOMS MED GZIGS MOR 'GYUR RAM SNYAM, ,ZHES BYA BAR SKABS KYI
TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O, ,SKAL LDAN RDZOGS BYANG SGRUBS PA'I NYE LA
MA MCHOG ,RIM GNYIS LAM

DANG MTSAN BCAS MTSAN MED KYIS, ,RNAL 'BYOR ZAB MO SGOM PA'I
SNOD RUNG DU, ,SGRUB PA'I DBANG BSKUR JI LTAR BYA BA'I TSUL,
,DKYIL CHOG RDOR 'PHRENG KRi YA SA MU TZTSA, ,GSANG SNGAGS LAM
RIM RNAMS LAS BSHAD PA BZHIN, ,DAM PA MANG

PO'I GSUNG GIS LEGS BSKUL BAS, ,SKAL MNYAM 'GA' YIS LAG TU BLANG
BDER BKOD, ,GZHUNG TSIG ZAB CING BRLING BAS RTOGS PAR DKA',
,BDAG NI BLO GROS SBYANGS PA SHIN TU DMAN, ,MA RTOGS LOG RTOGS
NOR 'KHRUL CI MCHIS PA, ,

@225A *, ,GZUR GNAS MKHAS PA RNAMS LA SNYING NAS BSHAGS, ,'DIR
'BAD DGE BA RDO RJE THEG PA'I CHOS, ,PHYOGS DUS KUN TU DAR ZHING
RGYAS PA DANG, ,'GRO KUN GSANG CHEN MYUR LAM LA BRTEN NAS, ,RDO
RJE 'CHANG DBANG MYUR DU 'THOB

PHYIR BSNGO, ,CES RDOR 'PHRENG NAS BSHAD PA'I DKYIL 'KHOR ZHE
GNYIS KRi YA NAS BSHAD PA'I DGE LEGS SU BYED PA'I DKYIL 'KHOR
GSUM STE DKYIL 'KHOR ZHE LNGA'I RAS BRIS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR DU
DBANG BSKUR BA'I DGA' DON GYI CHOG SGRIGS BLO GSAL MGUL ?

RGYAN NOR BU'I 'PHRENG BA ZHES BYA BA 'DI NI, MKHYEN RAB 'JAM
PA'I DBYANGS DANG GNYIS SU MED CING BRTZE BA 'JIG RTEN DBANG
PHYUG DANG DBYER MED PA'I DPAL LDAN BLA MA DAM PA, 'JAM MGON BLA
MA KHAMS GSUM CHOS KYI RGYAL PO'I RGYAL TSAB ZHE BZHI PA KHRI

RIN PO CHE NGAG DBANG BLO GROS RGYA MTSO DPAL BZANG PO'I ZHAL
SNGA NAS KYIS 'PHRENG BA'I DBANG BSKUR GCIG DANG, SNGAGS RIM SOR
BZHAG PA'I YIG CHA GCIG BYED YE THUB LTOS ZHES BKA'I GNANG BA
THOB CING, CHOS SDE CHEN PO DGON LUNG DU 'PHRENG BA'I DBANG
BSKUR SKABS

CHOS SDE'I KHRI RIN PO CHE DANG GZHI BYAS KYI DGE BA'I BSHES
GNYEN 'GA' ZHIG GIS BSKUL BA DANG, PHYIS SU MDO SNGAGS YONGS SU
RDZOGS PA'I BSTAN PA'I GSAL BYED MKHAS PA'I DBANG PO BSTAN
'GRO'I DON LA GCIG TU GZHOL BA'I DES PA DON GYI DGE BA'I

BSHES GNYEN BDE CHEN CHOS GLING GI KHRI RIN PO CHE GRAGS PA
RGYAL MTSAN, MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG LUG RGYA MTSO LTA BU LA THOS
BSAM BSGOM PA MTHAR PHYIN PA'I YONGS KYI DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN
CHEN PO DZA YA PAndI TA BLO BZANG 'PHRIN LAS, SDE SNOD

GSUM DANG RGYUD SDE BZHI'I THOS PA'I NOR GYIS PHYUG CING, SDOM
PA GSUM GYI BCAS 'TSAMS LAS MI 'DA' BAR BSTAN 'GRO'I DON KHUNG
DU KHYER BA'I RGYAL MKHAN PO RNAM RGYAL AER RDE NI NO MON HAN
MTSAN GZHAN BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS PHYOGS

LAS RNAM RGYAL, GSO PA RIG PA DANG NANG DON RIG PA LA SBYANGS PA
MI DMAN ZHING BSTAN 'GRO'I DON LA LHAG BSAM CHE BA'I RAB 'BYAMS
SMRA BA NGAG DBANG BSTAN 'DZIN AER DHI NI NO MON HAN, SDE SNOD
GSUM LA SBYANGS PA CHE

@225B ZHING MDO SNGAGS KYI LUNG MAN NGAG GIS PHYUG PA'I BKA'
'GYUR BA DO LON NOR GYI T'A BLA MA BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS SOGS
KYIS BSKUL PA LTAR BAN RGAN SNYOM LAS PA NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG
CHOS LDAN DPAL BZANG PO, ,

'JAM DBYANGS GONG MA'I LUNG GIS, KON TING PHU'U SHAN BKVANG TSI
T'A KOO SHRI MED GZHAN LCANG SKYA HU THOG THUR 'BOD PAS RNAL
'BYOR RDZOGS 'PHRENG, DKYIL CHOG RDO RJE 'PHRENG BA, KRi YA

SA MU NYTZA RJE BDAG NYID CHEN PO'I GSANG SNGAGS LAM RIM RNAMS
LA GZHI BYAS, SA BZANG 'PHAGS PA DANG PAn CHEN THAR RTZE BA
GNYIS KYIS MDZAD PA'I 'PHRENG BA DANG KRi YA SBRAGS MA'I SGRUB

DKYIL 'KHOR ? PAn CHEN BZANG BGRAS PAS MDZAD PA'I 'PHRENG BA
GNYIS KYI LHAN 'THABS, 'PHAGS SDE LO TZTSA BA CHAB MDO'I MKHAN
CHEN RJE DRUNG DGE 'DUN BKRA SHIS KYIS MDZAD

PA'I 'PHRENG BA DANG KRi YA SBRAGS MA'I SGRUB DKYIL, PAn CHEN
THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA'I RDZOGS 'PHRENG GI LHAN 'THABS, ZHAL SNGA
NAS BSAM SGANG PA MKHAN CHEN NGAG GI DBANG PO NGANG ZHAL

SNGA NAS RDO RJE 'DZIN PA DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSAN GYIS MDZAD PA'I
DBANG CHOG GI NGAG 'DON, SKYID SHOD ZHABS DRUG GIS MDZAD PA'I
'PHRENG BA DANG KRi YA SBRAGS MA'I SGRUB DKYIL

RNAMS KYI LEGS CHAS BRGYAN TE 'KHYER BDE BAR SBYAR BA'I YI GE PA
NI GZHUNG LUGS RAB 'BYAMS LA SBYANGS BA MI DMAN ZHING BSLAB GSUM
SDE SNOD 'DZIN PA'I RAB 'BYAMS SMRA BA BLO BZANG

NYI MA'O,, 'DIS KYANG RGYAL BSTAN SPYI DANG KHYAD PAR RGYAL BA
GNYIS PA 'JAM DPAL SNYING PO'I BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE DRI MA MED PA
'DI NYID PHYOGS DUS THAMS CAD DU DAR ZHING RGYAS LA YUN RING DU
GNAS PAR GYUR CIG
